                <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Founding Interns of League of Legends</span>
            </div>
            <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                    <img src="http://img.youtube.com/vi/N44R8c_F2lI/0.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                </div>
                <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Definitely (Not) Rivals | Riot Games documentary</span>
            </div>
            <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                    <img src="http://img.youtube.com/vi/l8ssa4YYfrg/0.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                </div>
                <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Interns Interviewing Interns</span>
            </div>
        </div>

    </div>

    <h1 class="c-heading">
        Level up @ Riot
    </h1>

    <hr class="c-rule">

    <p class="u-text-center">
        We’re helping players connect their passions to careers in gaming. Disciplines range from Game Design to Finance, Data Science to Art, Engineering to Brand Management and all that’s inbetween. Our university programs include internships for undergraduates and graduates, talks we give on campuses around the globe, graduate research projects we conduct in the winter, and classroom takeovers.
    </p>

    <div class="o-spacer"></div>

    <section class="o-section-bg">
        <h2 class="c-heading c-heading--left c-heading--light">Work Hard, Play Hard</h2>
        <p>
            That’s how many interns describe their time at Riot, and we think that’s pretty accurate. Interns roost in most Riot offices around the world, from LAX to Berlin, where they tackle tough problems while getting to know each other over rounds of League. We believe interns deserve the full-time Rioter treatment-- the opportunity to take on meaningful problems impacting over 70 million players rather than fetching coffee.
        </p>

        <div class="o-spacer"></div>

        <a href="http://www.riotgames.com/internship-info" class="c-button">Internship Information
            <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-button__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                <title>play-arrow</title>
                <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>
                <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
            </svg>
        </a>
    </section>

    <section class="o-section">

        <header class="o-section__header">
            <span class="o-section__top-text">Fun Fact #127</span>
            <h2 class="c-heading">All Random All Math</h2>
        </header>

        <div class="c-math-box clearfix">
            <div class="c-math-box__block">

    </section>

</div>

<div class="o-container o-container--full clearfix">

    <div class="o-grid o-grid--flex">

        <div class="o-grid__column o-grid__column--6-md">
            <div class="o-section-bg o-section-bg--compact o-section-bg--alt-1">
                <h2 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--spacer">Graduate Winter Project</h2>
                <hr class="c-rule">
                <p class="u-text-center">Our Graduate Winter Project invites a select number of graduate students to a Riot office to gain experience developing their business and analytical skills. It's a glimpse into the working life at Riot, so top students know what they'd be signing up for.</p>
                <p class="u-text-center">Each student team takes on the subject of a specific case study: challenging situations digging into key business decisions we face as a growing company. The small five- or six-person team learns our strategies and how we've applied them to similar problems. The objective and deliverables are set by Rioters who identify unique problem spaces for students to explore.</p>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="o-grid__column o-grid__column--6-md">
            <div class="o-section-bg o-section-bg--compact o-section-bg--alt-2 u-text-center">
                <div class="o-section-bg__logo c-logo c-logo--ulol">
                    uLoL
                </div>
                <p><strong>More than just a game.</strong></p>
                <p class="u-text-center">University League of Legends (ULoL) is a student-led network of League of Legends players on college campuses across the U.S. and Canada. Whether you’re new to League or a seasoned Rift vet, ULoL is your place to connect with other League players, learn how and why they play, and see what they're up to when afk.</p>
                <a href="https://www.youtube.com/embed/C5eqyn_g460?autoplay=1" class="c-image-thumb js-fancybox fancybox.iframe">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/ulol-thumb.jpg" alt="" class="c-image-thumb__image">
                    <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-image-thumb__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                        <title>play-arrow</title>
                        <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>

                    </svg>
                </a>
            </div>

                    </a>

<div id="content">

    <div class="o-container">

    <p class="u-text-center">Interns come from diverse backgrounds, studying all things A to Z: Applied Physics, Biology, Business (MBA), Computer Science, Economics, English, Entertainment Technology, Ethics, Illustration, International Business, Management & Information Systems, Politics, Religion, Social Psychology, Statistics—well, A to S, but we wouldn’t turn away a kickass Zoology major!</p>
    <p class="u-text-center">Interns nab honest mentorship during their time here. We work with awesome people and sharing knowledge is part of working here. You can also expect to level up while here: you'll unlock access to classes through Riot University to level up your skills while here. You'll share your hard work with all of Riot during the Intern Science Fair, when you’ll get feedback from other Rioters and see how far your work reaches when you learn how your project affects other teams.</p>
    <p class="u-text-center">Rioters tinker and build at our no holds barred 48hr internal hackathon <a href="http://thunderdome.riotgames.com/" target="_blank">Thunderdome</a>, where you can stretch the limits of your imagination and abilities.</p>
    <div class="o-spacer"></div>

    <section class="o-section-bg o-section-bg--compact o-section-bg--solid">

        <h2 class="c-heading c-heading--light">Perks of the Program?</h2>

        <div class="o-spacer o-spacer--small"></div>

        <ul class="c-list-grid clearfix">
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">PlayFund</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">You’ll sample a taste of this annual Rioter perk, with $150 to spend on videogames.
                    <a href="http://www.riotgames.com/articles/20121029/531/funding-riots-play" target="_blank">We use it to fuel our slavering hunger</a> to consume the newest and shiniest diversions; how you use it is up to you. Well, within reason. No matter how much you want it to, Monopoly doesn’t count. No, Matt, not even the Lord of the Rings Special Edition.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                    <title>play-arrow</title>
                    <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>
                    <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
                </svg>
            </li>
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">Housing</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">Building a community with fellow interns is part of the summer experience, so we shell out for local digs a brisk walk from our offices.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                    <title>play-arrow</title>
                    <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>
                    <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
                </svg>
            </li>
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">Riot University Classes</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">In addition to what you’ll learn from your team and day-to-day work, you can dive into Riot U classes and pick up some fresh leadership and self-awareness augments, or sign up for productivity coaching, professional moonsurfing tours, and more.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                    <title>play-arrow</title>
                    <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>
                    <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
                </svg>
            </li>
            <li class="c-list-grid__item">
                <h4 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-heading--left c-list-grid__title">Events</h4>
                <p class="c-list-grid__description">From coffee chats to lunch and learns to semi-regular mixers, there's plenty of ways to get to know your fellow Rioters.</p>
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 25 25" class="c-list-grid__icon c-icon c-icon--arrow">
                    <title>play-arrow</title>
                    <circle class="a" cx="12.5" cy="12.5" r="12.5"/>
                    <path class="b" d="M18 13l-9 5V8z"/>
                </svg>
            </li>
        </ul>
    </section>

    <div class="o-grid">

        <div class="o-grid__column o-grid__column--4-md">
            <h2 class="c-heading c-heading--left">Application Timeline</h2>
            <p>Because schools vary in their schedules so do we. Take care when applying and check application deadlines.</p>

            <a href="/riot-internships/faq" class="c-button">FAQ</a>
            <br><br>

            <p class="c-footnote">
                <span class="u-color-red">*</span>There's a record number of internship candidates this year, and we can't keep up! We want every applicant to have a good experience and get the attention they've earned, so we're temporarily shuttering internship applications for Software Engineering from January 9 until February 20.
            </p>
            <p class="c-footnote">
                Haven't applied yet but want to? Fret not! We'll be re-opening applications from February 20 until March 6.
            </p>

        </div>

        <div id="tabs-1" class="c-tabs__content">
            <p>Interns work on meaty projects with real impact, like pushing code to live servers, making impressively playful splash art, and building out a micro-feedback tool. You’ll gain hands-on experience working in games. Here’s just a sample of what interns have accomplished, often in under 14 weeks:</p>

                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            For my project this summer, I helped create the NA Scouting Grounds. In November, we'll be inviting the 20 best Challenger players from the NA ranked ladder to participate in a boot camp and showcase event in front of the pro LoL teams, in an esports version of a pro league scouting combine. This event is meant to be the stepping stone for players to go from being a ranked ladder climber to a LCS star.
                        </p>

                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Changerous</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            I worked on Changerous, an internal tool that creates an audit trail of changes made to services running in production. Because there are so many developers with production access, and so many different services running, it can be hard to track down why something is breaking, but Changerous will provide a centralized location where all recent changes can be collected and viewed.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-greg-k.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                    <div class="c-slider__content">

                        <div class="c-slider__header">
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <div class="c-slider__profile">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-greg-k.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Greg - Computer Science</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">LCU</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            This summer I worked on the League Client Update Alpha. Our team was responsible for building the Champion Detail Pages and the Landing Page. I worked on the layout and interface for the Skins tab of the Champion Details Page and the tech that allowed teams to customize landing pages in their regions. It was very rewarding to be able to deliver this improved experience to players.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-jerry-j.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                    <div class="c-slider__content">

                        <div class="c-slider__header">
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <div class="c-slider__profile">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-jerry-j.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-michael-a.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Jerry | Mike - Computer Science</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Insights Tech</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            We worked with the Insights Tech team to build the "real-time pipeline". Send any data to the pipeline, and we'll make sure it is stored and searchable within a second! RTP gives Riot Direct real-time visibility into every player's ping, while simultaneously processing the logs from the global fleet of LoL's platform servers. It was awesome to work on and own various parts of the highly-scalable service, from data ingestion to query performance.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="c-slider-nav c-slider-nav--no-margin">

                <div class="c-slider-nav__slider js-slider-nav" data-slider-tab="1">
                    <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                        <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                            <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/thumbs/thumb-grant-w.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                        </div>
                        <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Grant</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                        <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                            <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/thumbs/thumb-alex-m.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                        </div>
                        <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Alexander - Computer Science</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                        <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                            <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/thumbs/thumb-zack-e.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                        </div>
                        <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Zack - Psychology</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                        <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                            <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/thumbs/thumb-alex-v.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                        </div>
                        <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Alex - Computer Science</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                        <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                            <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/thumbs/thumb-greg-k.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                        </div>
                        <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Greg - Computer Science</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="c-slider-nav__slide">
                        <div class="c-slider-nav__thumb">
                            <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/thumbs/thumb-jerry-j.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider-nav__image">
                        </div>
                        <span class="c-slider-nav__title">Jerry | Mike - Computer Science</span>
                    </div>
                </div>

            </div>

        </div>
        <div id="tabs-2" class="c-tabs__content">
            <p>Interns work on meaty projects with real impact, like pushing code to live servers, making impressively playful splash art, and building out a micro-feedback tool. You’ll gain hands-on experience working in games. Here’s just a sample of what interns have accomplished, often in under 14 weeks:</p>

            <div class="c-slider c-slider--inner-content js-slider" data-slider-tab="2">
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-liu-l.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                    <div class="c-slider__content">

                        <div class="c-slider__header">
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <div class="c-slider__profile">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-liu-l.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Liu - Ph.D.</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Internal Segmentation Tool</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            Working at Riot is really exciting, it feels soooo different to work on something you care about. This project was not at all part of the projects arranged for me, but I saw a need, so I took the lead. At Riot, the culture of challenging convention to build new things really inspires me. I was working on player segmentation and realized there was a need to automate the process to make segmentation analysis more efficient for Researchers at Riot.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-michael-s.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                    <div class="c-slider__content">

                        <div class="c-slider__header">
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <div class="c-slider__profile">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-michael-s.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Michael - MBA</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Baker Pantheon</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            Having played League since Season 1, I was beyond excited to be a Brand Intern for the summer and build campaigns around my favorite champions. When I found out my projects would include Arcade and Baker Pantheon, I was even more psyched! From beginning to end, I was encouraged to participate in strategy discussions and make design decisions that impacted the player experience. I'll never forget directing Baker Pantheon's video, either!
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="c-slider__slide">
                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/slide-slyvia-k.jpg" alt="" class="c-slider__image">

                    <div class="c-slider__content">

                        <div class="c-slider__header">
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <div class="c-slider__profile">
                                    <img src="sites/all/modules/custom/riot/university_programs/img/slides/profile-sylvia-s.png" alt="" class="c-slider__portrait">
                                    <span class="c-slider__name">Sylvia - MBA</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="c-slider__block">
                                <h3 class="c-heading c-heading--light c-slider__heading">Advising setup for a multi-game future</h3>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <p class="c-slider__description">
                            As an MBA intern for Insights Analytics, I advised two groups at Riot on their strategic needs. My primary project was equipping a newly formed team (whose mission was to develop a platform for shared services across Riot's future games) with decision-making frameworks on what opportunities and products to prioritize. I also created the foundation for a dashboard showing game health metrics for Stonehearth and how their players were interacting with the game.
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>

            </div>

            <div class="c-slider-nav c-slider-nav--no-margin">

                <div class="c-slider-nav__slider js-slider-nav" data-slider-tab="2">

<h6 class="r7headline">

    <a id="main-content"></a>
            		<h1 class="title" id="page-title">Tours Faqs</h1>
                        <div class="block block-system block-main block-system-main odd block-without-title" id="block-system-main">
  <div class="block-inner clearfix">
                
    <div class="content clearfix">
      <article about="/tours/faqs" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" class="node node-page node-published node-not-promoted node-not-sticky author-jesse even clearfix" id="node-page-2137">
        <span property="dc:title" content="Tours Faqs" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>    
  
  <div class="content clearfix">
    <span class="print-link"></span><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"> <h3>
	Registration</h3>
<h6>
	<strong>Who can sign up for a tour?</strong></h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Tours are open to <em>League of Legends</em> players who are level 30 or higher, and all visitors must be 13 years of age or older to sign up for tours</li>
	<li>
		Anyone between 13 and 17 years of age must be accompanied by a parent/legal guardian and will be required to submit their information when signing up</li>
	<li>
		If you require a parent/legal guardian in attendance, they aren&#39;t required to be a <em>League </em>player</li>
	<li>
		If you&#39;re with the press, please don&#39;t sign up for a tour -- we want to keep these spaces open for players. We can help you out separately if you contact <a href="http://mailto:media@riotgames.com">media@riotgames.com</a></li>
</ul>
<h6>
	<strong>What do I need to know before signing up?</strong></h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Each visitor must fill out the registration form - no exceptions</li>
	<li>
		You&rsquo;ll need to submit one form of legal identification that matches your legal name, which you&rsquo;ll also need to bring on the day of your tour; you can submit a:
		<ul>
			<li>
				Driver license</li>
			<li>
				Government-issued Identification card</li>
			<li>
				Passport (required for all non-US citizens)</li>
		</ul>
	</li>
	<li>
		Visitors must be level 30 in <em>League of Legends</em> in order to be considered for the tour (<em>parents/guardians exempt</em>)&nbsp;</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	<strong>Can I register my friend as my parent/guardian?</strong></h6>
<div>
	<ul>
		<li>
			Nope! Each visitor must register independently&nbsp;</li>
	</ul>
</div>
<ul>
</ul>
<h6>
	<strong>I am a minor, and I want to come with a friend who is a minor. Do we both need to have our own parent/guardian with us, or can we come with just one parent/guardian?</strong></h6>
<div>
	<ul>
		<li>
			Each minor must be accompanied by their own legal parent/guardian</li>
	</ul>
</div>
<h6>
	I have someone giving me a ride to campus, can they accompany me on the tour?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Anyone planning on attending the tour needs to register and be confirmed for the tour</li>
</ul>
<div>
	<ul>
	</ul>
</div>
<h6>
	<strong>How often does Riot offer tours?</strong></h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Tours are limited and released on a monthly basis, so check back often!</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	<strong>How do I register for a tour?</strong></h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Check out the tour scheduler <a href="/tours/schedule">here</a></li>
	<li>
		Please only sign up for ONE tour. If you register for multiple tours, you&#39;ll be removed from the system</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Is there a fee to sign up?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Nope! Riot HQ tours are free of charge</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	How do I know if I&rsquo;m confirmed?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		You&rsquo;ll receive a confirmation receipt for your registration within three business days (Note: registering doesn&rsquo;t guarantee attendance)</li>
	<li>
		Attendance is confirmed based on availability on a first come first serve basis; we may review in-game behavior, if you&rsquo;ve visited us before, etc.</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	I was denied registration, how long before I can register for a tour again?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		You&rsquo;ll need to wait 30 days before signing up for another tour. However, if any negative chats/behavior remain in your recent history, you may still be denied after the 30 days have passed. For further inquiries on how to improve your status, consult <a href="https://support.riotgames.com/hc/en-us" target="_blank">Player Support</a></li>
</ul>
<h6>
	I was denied registration due to a negative report in game play, but I don&#39;t have a ban from the game currently. Why can&#39;t I register?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		There are specific requirements in place for tours which may be more restrictive than game play. A player may have recent negative chats containing derogatory or aggressive language in gameplay that would prevent the player from being able to participate in tours, even if they&#39;re not banned from the game</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Is the tour wheelchair-accessible?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Yes! You&rsquo;ll be able to notify us when filling out your registration</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	What if I have a younger brother/sister who is under 13? Can they not come?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Our <a href="http://na.leagueoflegends.com/en/legal/termsofuse" target="_blank">Terms of Use for <em>League of Legends</em></a> states that the site and game aren&rsquo;t directed to children under 13 years of age; due to <a href="http://www.coppa.org/coppa.htm" target="_blank">COPPA-compliance reasons</a>, we won&rsquo;t be offering tours to children under 13 years of age at this time</li>
</ul>
<h3>
	&nbsp;</h3>
<h3>
	Getting There</h3>
<h6>
	Where is Riot HQ located?&nbsp;</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		We&rsquo;re located in <a href="http://www.riotgames.com/articles/20150423/1660/%E2%80%98twas-night-our-move-la" target="_blank">Los Angeles, California</a></li>
</ul>
<h6>
	How do I get there?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		We&rsquo;ll share details and directions with confirmed tour attendees via email</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Is there parking?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Yes, there will be free visitor parking available</li>
</ul>
<h3>
	&nbsp;</h3>
<h3>
	For The Tour</h3>
<h6>
	What do I need to bring?&nbsp;</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		A legal form of identification (the same as you submitted when signing up)</li>
	<li>
		A parent or legal guardian if you&rsquo;re under the age of 18</li>
	<li>
		Wear comfortable shoes (there are breaks and seated portions, but you&rsquo;ll be walking the campus)</li>
	<li>
		Hats and sunscreen if it&rsquo;s sunny out</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	What shouldn&rsquo;t I bring?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Backpacks, luggage, large purses, or oversized bags</li>
	<li>
		Animals or pets (although seeing eye dogs and service dogs are welcome, just give us a heads-up)</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	How long is the tour?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		<div>
			You should expect to carve out three to three and a half hours for a Riot HQ tour</div>
	</li>
	<li>
		<div>
			If you&rsquo;re getting a ride from someone not attending the tour, please plan accordingly, only confirmed registrants will be permitted to park on campus</div>
	</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	What will I see on the tour?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		You&rsquo;ll get an inside look into our studio, taking you through our PC Bang, esports building, and other areas that&rsquo;ll give you a taste of how Rioters spend their days. You&rsquo;ll also get an inside look into Riot culture, including how League and the community influenced the design of our space</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Do other Riot offices offer tours?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Right now, tours are only offered at Riot HQ in Los Angeles. If we begin to offer tours of other offices, we&rsquo;ll be sure to share updates here</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Will I get to meet any Rioters?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		You&rsquo;ll see lots of Rioters from different teams, and maybe even meet a couple, but there won&rsquo;t be any extended meet and greets during the tour</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Is there a gift store I can buy merch from while I&rsquo;m there?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		The Merch Store is only open during LCS matches, but you can <a href="https://na.merch.riotgames.com/en/" target="_blank">shop online here</a></li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Will I get to see the LCS Studio?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Yes! You&rsquo;ll get a peek inside the Battle Arena (as long as there&rsquo;s no filming going on), backstage areas, and other highlights in our esports building</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	Are the tours given in different languages?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Currently tours are in English only</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	I have a group that&rsquo;s interested in a tour, what should I do?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		To offer the best tour experience, we try to keep tour groups small; we aren&rsquo;t taking group requests at this time, but keep an eye on this page for updates</li>
</ul>
<h6>
	What if I can&rsquo;t make it anymore or I&#39;m going to be late?</h6>
<ul>
	<li>
		Let us know as soon as you can; we&rsquo;d prefer that you cancel instead of not showing</li>
	<li>
		If you&#39;re going to be late, please contact us ASAP. Please be advised that we cannot accept anyone that is more than 15 minutes late as it causes disruption for the rest of the tour guests</li>
	<li>
		Please be sure to account for Los Angeles traffic and leave a buffer as accidents, traffic jams, construction, etc are common</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>Questions? Contact <a href="mailto:riothqtours@riotgames.com">riothqtours@riotgames.com&nbsp;</a></strong></p>
 </div></div></div>  </div>

    <a id="main-content"></a>
            		<h1 class="title" id="page-title">Riot's making a move</h1>
                        <div class="block block-system block-main block-system-main odd block-without-title" id="block-system-main">
  <div class="block-inner clearfix">
                
    <div class="content clearfix">
      


<article about="/articles/20131107/983/riots-making-move" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" class="node node-article node-published node-not-promoted node-not-sticky author-sschutz odd clearfix" id="node-article-983">
        <span property="dc:title" content="Riot&#039;s making a move" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span><span property="sioc:num_replies" content="0" datatype="xsd:integer" class="rdf-meta element-hidden"></span>	  
    
    <div class="post-date">Posted on 11-07-13</div>		
		<div class="share-bar">
			<a class="print_ico" href="/print/articles/20131107/983/riots-making-move">Print</a>
			<!-- <a class="pdf_ico" href="/printpdf/articles/20131107/983/riots-making-move">PDF</a> -->
			<span class='st_email_custom st_ico' displayText='Email'></span>
			<span class='st_twitter_custom st_ico' displayText='Tweet'></span>
			<span class='st_facebook_custom st_ico' displayText='Facebook'></span>
			<span class='st_linkedin_custom st_ico' displayText='LinkedIn'></span>
			<span class='st_google_custom st_ico' displayText='Google'></span>
			<script type="text/javascript">var switchTo5x=true;</script>
			<script type="text/javascript" src="http://w.sharethis.com/button/buttons.js"></script>
			<script type="text/javascript">
				stLight.options({
		        publisher: 'f65a6e51-8a93-4acd-a665-976809c16a17',
		        onhover: false
		    });</script>
		</div>

    
  
  <div class="content clearfix">
    <div class="field field-name-field-main-image field-type-image field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><img typeof="foaf:Image" src="http://www.riotgames.com/sites/default/files/styles/article_image/public/content/article/images/main/ElementLA.png?itok=laJS1RSw" width="700" height="300" alt="ElementLA" /></div></div></div><div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"> <p>Over the last year, things have gotten a little too cozy at Riot HQ in Santa Monica. As we&rsquo;ve grown, we&rsquo;ve squeezed ourselves into every cranny and we&rsquo;ve spread across multiple floors and buildings, making communication between teams occasionally tough. But when talk turned to <a href="http://blogs.zappos.com/blogs/inside-zappos/2009/04/01/bunkdesks">bunk desking</a> as a solution for our space woes, we got serious about looking for a larger, more contiguous space to host us all.</p>
<p>We&rsquo;ve found our next home. Known as <a href="http://elementla.com/">ElementLA</a>, Riot&rsquo;s new home sits less than a mile east of our current digs &ndash; still just a few klicks from the ocean, but nicely situated next to a soon-to-open metro station that&rsquo;ll be able to whisk Rioters to downtown LA and beyond. We&rsquo;ll move in spring 2015.&nbsp;</p>
<p>We&rsquo;re stoked. The creature comforts will be upgraded: no more lines in the bathrooms, shorter waits at the Starbucks machines, and definitely no more threats of bunk desking. Basically, we&rsquo;re gonna be running short on first-world problems for a while.</p>
<p>More seriously, though, this move represents an investment in Riot&rsquo;s work environment that&rsquo;s consistent with our belief that a fun, comfortable place to work enhances creativity, productivity and communication between teams.</p>
<p>We put a lot of effort into shaping our office environment because we believe that it shapes us and the stuff we develop. Sure, in our early years, Riot managed to launch <em>League of Legends</em> from a space where the ceiling leaked and where &ldquo;conference room 2&rdquo; consisted of a whiteboard propped in a fire escape stairwell. But we&rsquo;ve always admired visionary companies like Pixar and Google who invest in bodaciously productive workspaces. We aren&rsquo;t looking to pile on gold-plated perks, just mercilessly crush space issues to create a playful, comfortable, and collaborative space where we can do our very best work.</p>
<p>So back to today&rsquo;s news. Here are the facts: we&rsquo;ve signed a lease. We&rsquo;re looking to move all Santa Monica Rioters (with room for growth) into the new space in the first half of 2015. We&rsquo;ll post plenty of photos when there&rsquo;s something interesting to look at.&nbsp;</p>
 </div></div></div>
        
    <span class="print-link"></span><div class="field-group-format group_tags field-group-div group-tags clearfix speed-none effect-none"><h3><span>Tags:</span></h3><div class="field field-name-field-topic field-type-taxonomy-term-reference field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><a href="/topic/riot-news" typeof="skos:Concept" property="rdfs:label skos:prefLabel">Riot in the News</a></div><div class="field-item odd"><a href="/topic/rioter-perks" typeof="skos:Concept" property="rdfs:label skos:prefLabel">Rioter Perks</a></div><div class="field-item even"><a href="/categories/category" typeof="skos:Concept" property="rdfs:label skos:prefLabel">Working @ Riot Games</a></div></div></div><div class="field field-name-field-tags field-type-taxonomy-term-reference field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><a href="/tags/focus-talent-team" typeof="skos:Concept" property="rdfs:label skos:prefLabel">Focus on talent &amp; team</a></div></div></div></div><div class="field field-name-field-office-location-tag field-type-taxonomy-term-reference field-label-inline clearfix"><div class="field-label">Office Location:&nbsp;</div><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><a href="/office-locations/los-angeles" typeof="skos:Concept" property="rdfs:label skos:prefLabel">Los Angeles</a></div></div></div>  </div>
